<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user's goal is to build a comprehensive Offline-First Electron Agent for Windows 11 tablets.

PRODUCT REQUIREMENTS:
- An Electron-based agent application with role-based access (Normal User PIN: 3842, Admin PIN: 9988).
- The agent must access hardware (USB scanners) and run as a background process with a System Tray icon.
- It must collect and display extensive system information, visible only to admins.
- The system must support multiple tenants. An admin should be able to select a tenant (e.g., Europcar) and see all associated locations and devices, sourced from a central MongoDB Atlas database.
- The agent must use a local SQLite database for offline data storage, which synchronizes with the central MongoDB Atlas database.
- The agent should support a self-setup flow, including manual selection (Continent -> Country -> City -> Location -> Device) and an Activation Code flow (QR code scanning).
- An admin portal () for managing tenants, locations, devices, and generating activation codes.
- A fully automated, one-click build script () is required for easy installation.
- The application and installer should be branded with a custom logo.
- A complete **Location Lifecycle Management** system to manage statuses (, , ).
- A complete **Device Lifecycle Management** system to track the entire history of every piece of hardware (devices, docking stations), including purchase date, warranty, assignments, status changes, manufacturer, model, OS, and software version.
- A comprehensive **Import/Export functionality** (CSV/Excel) and **dynamic column management** for all data tables within the application.

**User's preferred language**: German

**what currently exists?**
A full-stack application with a React frontend and a FastAPI backend, featuring a web-based Admin Portal.

Recent key features implemented include:
-   **Bug Fix:** A critical navigation bug in the Admin Portal that made tabs unresponsive has been resolved. The UI now correctly uses URL-based routing.
-   **Universal Table Features:** A comprehensive import/export system (CSV/Excel) and a dynamic column manager (show/hide/reorder) have been implemented across most major data tables (, , , , , etc.) using a new set of reusable UI components.
-   **Performance Overhaul:** Significant performance enhancements have been implemented. The backend now automatically creates database indexes on startup. The frontend uses pagination, skeleton loading screens, and in some cases, list virtualization () to handle large datasets efficiently.
-   **UI/UX Improvements:** The global search bar and its suggestions dropdown have been widened, and the Sync button has been removed from the header per user request.

**Last working item**:
-   **Last item agent was working:** Addressing a user's confusion about why no devices were available when creating a new Kit. The agent diagnosed that devices must have a status of in_storage and be unassigned to a kit. The agent began implementing a three-part solution: 1) A new Storage Overview page, 2) Improved UI hints and a direct link within the Create Kit modal, 3) An easier workflow for getting new devices into storage.
-   **Status:** IN PROGRESS

**Code Architecture**


**Key Technical Concepts**
-   **URL-Driven State:** The navigation bug fix reinforced using the URL () as the single source of truth for view state, not internal component state.
-   **Component-Based Architecture:** Cross-cutting concerns like data export, pagination, and column settings were abstracted into highly reusable UI components, promoting DRY principles.
-   **Frontend Performance Patterns:** A suite of optimization techniques was implemented: pagination (reducing initial data load), skeleton UIs (improving perceived speed), and virtualization (rendering only visible rows).
-   **Backend Performance Patterns:** Using database indexes is a fundamental optimization to accelerate data retrieval, implemented here via an automated script on server startup.
